          </article>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </div>
      </div>

           </a>
          </h3>

          EYEWITNESS: Stephen Glass proved he was the real thing after winning Coca-Cola bike at Hampden
         </a>
        </h3>
        <p class="post__excerpt">

				/** If 'a' tags with 'target="_blank"' don't have 'data-processed="true"' */
				if ( ! target_blank.data( 'processed', 'true' ) ) {
					/** Apply the rel="noopener" */
					target_blank.attr('rel', 'noopener');

					const el = $(this);

					let out = window.open();
					out.opener = null;
					out.location = el.attr('href');

					e.preventDefault();
				});
			});
